Caretta’s experienced team provides customized solutions for its partners using cutting edge software techniques which involves applying global standards.  Caretta is a Microsoft Gold Cerftified Partner since 1998.

We understand the enterprise and its direction, the complexities of the business needs, company processes, operation systems and the priorities. Regarding the analysis, We offer technology solutions that provide business value and turn-key software projects for the business needs.

We are software solution leader in Turkey Pharmaceutical Sector and our target is exporting own software solutions to EMEA region which prepared within global quality standards. We listed within our rising progress in “Technology Fast 50 Turkey” and  “Technology Fast 500 EMEA” by Deloitte at 2014 and 2015.
